                   1200 cm from the sample. The angle separation  2266600100026

               Length 2.54 cm (D1)/ 5.08 cm (D2-D5).              2266600100029 
               The angle region covered is 12.5 deg to 160 deg.   2266600100030

               fluence monitor, diameter 3.81 cm, length 3.81 cm. 2266600100032 
               The movable monitor (in a fixed distance of 651 cm)2266600100033

CORRECTIONS     Monte Carlo simulated TOF spectra of the complete 2266600100042 
                angular distribution were iteratively adjusted to 2266600100043 
                the measured TOF spectra. The simulation comprised2266600100044

                scattering geometry between target, sample and    2266600100046 
                detectors.                                        2266600100047 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T)  Total errors comprise counting statistics and 2266600100048 
                systematic contributions of                       2266600100049 
           (ERR-1)    Error due to detector efficiency (2%),      2266600100050 
           (ERR-2)    Error due to   angle uncert. (0.2 deg),     2266600100051 
           (MONIT-ERR)  Error due to    n-p scattering (1%),      2266600100052 
           (ERR-3) Error due to multiple scattering correct. (5%).2266600100053 
                Some inelastic angle-integrated cross sections    2266600100054 
                contain an additional uncertainty component of    2266600100055 
                between 1.2% and 17% in order to consider the     2266600100056 
                influence of the chosen maximum order L-max       2266600100057 
                of the fitted Legendre polynomial on the integral 2266600100058 
                cross section (see also report PTB-N-43).         2266600100059
